Mindi is considered to be a game for smart people and needs some strategy to win it.\r\n\r\nMindi is designed for four players playing in two partnerships. The game uses a standard 52 card deck. The ranking of the cards in this deck are as follows (from high to low); Ace, King, Queen, Jack, 10, 9, 8, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2. \r\n\r\nThe player who draws the highest card of all would be designated the first dealer. \r\n\r\nThe dealer shuffles the cards and deals the hand. He deals out 13 card hands around the table. \r\n\r\nGame is split into two modes:\r\n\r\nHide Mode- The player to the dealer’s right selects a card placing it to table face down which will be declared as trump suit for that play.\r\n\r\nCut Mode- Play begins without choosing trump suit when the player is unable to follow the suit then whichever he/she chooses becomes the trump of the deal.\r\n\r\nThus, once a trump suit is designated for the hand, the highest card of the trump suit played to the trick wins the trick. If no trump card has been played to the trick, the highest card of the suit led wins the trick. The winner of each trick leads the first card to the next trick. Each captured trick should be kept in a face down pile of cards, gathered by the winner of the trick. \r\n\r\nAfter all 13 tricks have been played the captured cards are then examined to determine the winner of the hand. \r\n\r\nIf one partnership manages to capture three or four of the Tens, they win the hand.
